function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 23') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.23!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// File added: Acknowledgements.txt
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('Acknowledgements.txt', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('DQpNb3N0IG9mIHRoZSBpY29ucyBhcmUgdGFrZW4gZnJvbSB0aGUNCk51dm9sYSBpY29uIHBhY2sgYnkgRGF2aWQgVmlnbm9uaSwNCmxpY2Vuc2VkIHVuZGVyIHRoZSB0ZXJtcyBvZiBHTlUvTEdQTC4NCg0KaHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuaWNvbmZpbmRlci5jb20vaWNvbnNl'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('dHMvbnV2b2xhMg0KaHR0cHM6Ly9maW5kaWNvbnMuY29tL3BhY2svMjExOC9udXZvbGENCg=='));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('Acknowledgements.txt') && (sha1_file('Acknowledgements.txt') != 'c20c82a7aeb7e26460b1d8cf94ee907d2aa46120')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: Acknowledgements.txt');
	$tmp = pathinfo('Acknowledgements.txt');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('Acknowledgements.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('Acknowledgements.txt', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('Acknowledgements.txt')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): Acknowledgements.txt');
} else if (sha1_file('Acknowledgements.txt') != 'c20c82a7aeb7e26460b1d8cf94ee907d2aa46120') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): Acknowledgements.txt');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('Acknowledgements.txt', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of Acknowledgements.txt');
}

if (is_file('img/admin_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/admin_big.png') != '813184dba3a88435bdf45f11f5d5d5eee83ec9e3')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/admin_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/admin_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/admin_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/admin_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_2();
if (!is_file('img/admin_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/admin_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/admin_big.png') != '813184dba3a88435bdf45f11f5d5d5eee83ec9e3') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/admin_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/admin_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/admin_big.png');
}

if (is_file('img/login_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/login_big.png') != '857081d550e5f0e0150ebdaeca11fe35e4de124b')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/login_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/login_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/login_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/login_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_3();
if (!is_file('img/login_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/login_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/login_big.png') != '857081d550e5f0e0150ebdaeca11fe35e4de124b') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/login_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/login_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/login_big.png');
}

if (is_file('img/ra_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/ra_big.png') != '8acb55c99a1c44aa61b82575f862e9dbcdf3c84a')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/ra_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/ra_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/ra_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/ra_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_4();
if (!is_file('img/ra_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/ra_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/ra_big.png') != '8acb55c99a1c44aa61b82575f862e9dbcdf3c84a') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/ra_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/ra_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/ra_big.png');
}

if (is_file('img/system_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/system_big.png') != 'd27b41f4ae08708dbfe31ecc0b05daba7000d231')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/system_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/system_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/system_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/system_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_5();

	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/system_big.png');

	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/system_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/system_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/system_big.png');
}

if (is_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/treeicon.png') && (sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/treeicon.png') != 'bb5e11878412bf27273dc707066aec8440611ea4')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/treeicon.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/treeicon.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/treeicon.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/treeicon.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_11();
if (!is_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/treeicon.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/treeicon.png');

	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/treeicon.png');
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: action.php');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('action.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): action.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('action.php') != 'ff4da4d1173cc8ef203e8e089181e57a25e0352e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): action.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('action.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of action.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'ff4da4d1173cc8ef203e8e089181e57a25e0352e') {
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== '2b9e2847592ea422fc7575f4b92dafc087d2a499') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: action.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('action.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('action.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('action.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'ff4da4d1173cc8ef203e8e089181e57a25e0352e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): action.php');
		}
	}
}

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/900_contact_admin/treeicon.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/900_contact_admin/treeicon.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/900_contact_admin/treeicon.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/900_contact_admin/treeicon.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_26();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/900_contact_admin/treeicon.png') !== '2e449821f59484f5ec0b944aededa303af987d52') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/900_contact_admin/treeicon.png');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 24\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 24') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
